\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{comment}{/* Note about libpng version numbers:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{comment}{ *    Due to various miscommunications, unforeseen code incompatibilities}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{comment}{ *    and occasional factors outside the authors' control, version numbering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{comment}{ *    on the library has not always been consistent and straightforward.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{comment}{ *    The following table summarizes matters since version 0.89c, which was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{195 \textcolor{comment}{ *    the first widely used release:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{196 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{197 \textcolor{comment}{ *    source                 png.h  png.h  shared-\/lib}}
\DoxyCodeLine{198 \textcolor{comment}{ *    version                string   int  version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{comment}{ *    -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/                -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/  -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.89c "{}1.0 beta 3"{}     0.89      89  1.0.89}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.90  "{}1.0 beta 4"{}     0.90      90  0.90  [should have been 2.0.90]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.95  "{}1.0 beta 5"{}     0.95      95  0.95  [should have been 2.0.95]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.96  "{}1.0 beta 6"{}     0.96      96  0.96  [should have been 2.0.96]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.97b "{}1.00.97 beta 7"{} 1.00.97   97  1.0.1 [should have been 2.0.97]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.97c                  0.97      97  2.0.97}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.98                   0.98      98  2.0.98}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.99                   0.99      98  2.0.99}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{comment}{ *    0.99a-\/m                0.99      99  2.0.99}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.00                   1.00     100  2.1.0 [100 should be 10000]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.0      (from here on, the   100  2.1.0 [100 should be 10000]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.1       png.h string is   10001  2.1.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.1a-\/e    identical to the  10002  from here on, the shared library}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.2       source version)   10002  is 2.V where V is the source code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.2a-\/b                      10003  version, except as noted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.3                         10003}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.3a-\/d                      10004}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.4                         10004}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.4a-\/f                      10005}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.5 (+ 2 patches)           10005}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.5a-\/d                      10006}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.5e-\/r                      10100 (not source compatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.5s-\/v                      10006 (not binary compatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.6 (+ 3 patches)           10006 (still binary incompatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.6d-\/f                      10007 (still binary incompatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.6g                        10007}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.6h                        10007  10.6h (testing xy.z so-\/numbering)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.6i                        10007  10.6i}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.6j                        10007  2.1.0.6j (incompatible with 1.0.0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.7beta11-\/14        DLLNUM  10007  2.1.0.7beta11-\/14 (binary compatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.7beta15-\/18           1    10007  2.1.0.7beta15-\/18 (binary compatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.7rc1-\/2               1    10007  2.1.0.7rc1-\/2 (binary compatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.7                    1    10007  (still compatible)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{ *    ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.0.69                  10    10069  10.so.0.69[.0]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{ *    ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.2.59                  13    10259  12.so.0.59[.0]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{ *    ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.4.20                  14    10420  14.so.0.20[.0]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{ *    ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.5.30                  15    10530  15.so.15.30[.0]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{ *    ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{ *    1.6.37                  16    10637  16.so.16.37[.0]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{ *    Henceforth the source version will match the shared-\/library major and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{ *    minor numbers; the shared-\/library major version number will be used for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{ *    changes in backward compatibility, as it is intended.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{ *    The PNG\_LIBPNG\_VER macro, which is not used within libpng but is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{ *    available for applications, is an unsigned integer of the form XYYZZ}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{ *    corresponding to the source version X.Y.Z (leading zeros in Y and Z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{ *    Beta versions were given the previous public release number plus a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{ *    letter, until version 1.0.6j; from then on they were given the upcoming}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{ *    public release number plus "{}betaNN"{} or "{}rcNN"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{ *    Binary incompatibility exists only when applications make direct access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{ *    to the info\_ptr or png\_ptr members through png.h, and the compiled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{ *    application is loaded with a different version of the library.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{ *    DLLNUM will change each time there are forward or backward changes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{ *    in binary compatibility (e.g., when a new feature is added).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{ * See libpng.txt or libpng.3 for more information.  The PNG specification}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{ * is available as a W3C Recommendation and as an ISO/IEC Standard; see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{ * <https://www.w3.org/TR/2003/REC-\/PNG-\/20031110/>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 }
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 }
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{/* This is not the place to learn how to use libpng. The file libpng-\/manual.txt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{ * describes how to use libpng, and the file example.c summarizes it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{ * with some code on which to build.  This file is useful for looking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{ * at the actual function definitions and structure components.  If that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 \textcolor{comment}{ * file has been stripped from your copy of libpng, you can find it at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{ * <http://www.libpng.org/pub/png/libpng-\/manual.txt>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{ * If you just need to read a PNG file and don't want to read the documentation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{ * skip to the end of this file and read the section entitled 'simplified API'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 }

\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_LIBPNG\_VER\_STRING "{}1.6.37"{}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{314 \textcolor{comment}{/* Careful here.  At one time, Guy wanted to use 082, but that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315 \textcolor{comment}{ * would be octal.  We must not include leading zeros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316 \textcolor{comment}{ * Versions 0.7 through 1.0.0 were in the range 0 to 100 here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317 \textcolor{comment}{ * (only version 1.0.0 was mis-\/numbered 100 instead of 10000).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318 \textcolor{comment}{ * From version 1.0.1 it is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319 \textcolor{comment}{ * XXYYZZ, where XX=major, YY=minor, ZZ=release}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_LIBPNG\_VER 10637 }\textcolor{comment}{/* 1.6.37 */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{378 \textcolor{comment}{/* This file is arranged in several sections:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{379 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{380 \textcolor{comment}{ * 1. [omitted]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{381 \textcolor{comment}{ * 2. Any configuration options that can be specified by for the application}}
\DoxyCodeLine{382 \textcolor{comment}{ *    code when it is built.  (Build time configuration is in pnglibconf.h)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{383 \textcolor{comment}{ * 3. Type definitions (base types are defined in pngconf.h), structure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{384 \textcolor{comment}{ *    definitions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{385 \textcolor{comment}{ * 4. Exported library functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{386 \textcolor{comment}{ * 5. Simplified API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{387 \textcolor{comment}{ * 6. Implementation options.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{388 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{389 \textcolor{comment}{ * The library source code has additional files (principally pngpriv.h) that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{390 \textcolor{comment}{ * allow configuration of the library.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{391 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{392 }
\DoxyCodeLine{393 \textcolor{comment}{/* Section 1: [omitted] */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{394 }
\DoxyCodeLine{395 \textcolor{comment}{/* Section 2: run time configuration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{396 \textcolor{comment}{ * See pnglibconf.h for build time configuration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{397 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{398 \textcolor{comment}{ * Run time configuration allows the application to choose between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{399 \textcolor{comment}{ * implementations of certain arithmetic APIs.  The default is set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{400 \textcolor{comment}{ * at build time and recorded in pnglibconf.h, but it is safe to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{401 \textcolor{comment}{ * override these (and only these) settings.  Note that this won't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{402 \textcolor{comment}{ * change what the library does, only application code, and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{403 \textcolor{comment}{ * settings can (and probably should) be made on a per-\/file basis}}
\DoxyCodeLine{404 \textcolor{comment}{ * by setting the \#defines before including png.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{405 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{406 \textcolor{comment}{ * Use macros to read integers from PNG data or use the exported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{407 \textcolor{comment}{ * functions?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{408 \textcolor{comment}{ *   PNG\_USE\_READ\_MACROS: use the macros (see below)  Note that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{409 \textcolor{comment}{ *     the macros evaluate their argument multiple times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{410 \textcolor{comment}{ *   PNG\_NO\_USE\_READ\_MACROS: call the relevant library function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{411 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{412 \textcolor{comment}{ * Use the alternative algorithm for compositing alpha samples that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{413 \textcolor{comment}{ * does not use division?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{414 \textcolor{comment}{ *   PNG\_READ\_COMPOSITE\_NODIV\_SUPPORTED: use the 'no division'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{415 \textcolor{comment}{ *      algorithm.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{416 \textcolor{comment}{ *   PNG\_NO\_READ\_COMPOSITE\_NODIV: use the 'division' algorithm.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{417 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{418 \textcolor{comment}{ * How to handle benign errors if PNG\_ALLOW\_BENIGN\_ERRORS is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{419 \textcolor{comment}{ * false?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{420 \textcolor{comment}{ *   PNG\_ALLOW\_BENIGN\_ERRORS: map calls to the benign error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{421 \textcolor{comment}{ *      APIs to png\_warning.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{422 \textcolor{comment}{ * Otherwise the calls are mapped to png\_error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{423 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{424 }
\DoxyCodeLine{425 \textcolor{comment}{/* Section 3: type definitions, including structures and compile time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{426 \textcolor{comment}{ * constants.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{427 \textcolor{comment}{ * See pngconf.h for base types that vary by machine/system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{428 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{429 }

\DoxyCodeLine{446 \textcolor{comment}{/* png\_info contains information read from or to be written to a PNG file.  One}}
\DoxyCodeLine{447 \textcolor{comment}{ * or more of these must exist while reading or creating a PNG file.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{448 \textcolor{comment}{ * information is not used by libpng during read but is used to control what}}
\DoxyCodeLine{449 \textcolor{comment}{ * gets written when a PNG file is created.  "{}png\_get\_"{} function calls read}}
\DoxyCodeLine{450 \textcolor{comment}{ * information during read and "{}png\_set\_"{} functions calls write information}}
\DoxyCodeLine{451 \textcolor{comment}{ * when creating a PNG.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{452 \textcolor{comment}{ * been moved into a separate header file that is not accessible to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{453 \textcolor{comment}{ * applications.  Read libpng-\/manual.txt or libpng.3 for more info.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{454 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{459 }
\DoxyCodeLine{460 \textcolor{comment}{/* Types with names ending 'p' are pointer types.  The corresponding types with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{461 \textcolor{comment}{ * names ending 'rp' are identical pointer types except that the pointer is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{462 \textcolor{comment}{ * marked 'restrict', which means that it is the only pointer to the object}}
\DoxyCodeLine{463 \textcolor{comment}{ * passed to the function.  Applications should not use the 'restrict' types;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{464 \textcolor{comment}{ * it is always valid to pass 'p' to a pointer with a function argument of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{465 \textcolor{comment}{ * corresponding 'rp' type.  Different compilers have different rules with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{466 \textcolor{comment}{ * regard to type matching in the presence of 'restrict'.  For backward}}
\DoxyCodeLine{467 \textcolor{comment}{ * compatibility libpng callbacks never have 'restrict' in their parameters and,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{468 \textcolor{comment}{ * consequentially, writing portable application code is extremely difficult if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{469 \textcolor{comment}{ * an attempt is made to use 'restrict'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{470 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{471 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \mbox{\hyperlink{structpng__struct__def}{png\_struct}} * \mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_af21b002e402fd844f1767dc3e7e92756}{PNG\_RESTRICT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{514 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{547 \textcolor{comment}{/* png\_text holds the contents of a text/ztxt/itxt chunk in a PNG file,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{548 \textcolor{comment}{ * and whether that contents is compressed or not.  The "{}key"{} field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{549 \textcolor{comment}{ * points to a regular zero-\/terminated C string.  The "{}text"{} fields can be a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{550 \textcolor{comment}{ * regular C string, an empty string, or a NULL pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{551 \textcolor{comment}{ * However, the structure returned by png\_get\_text() will always contain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{552 \textcolor{comment}{ * the "{}text"{} field as a regular zero-\/terminated C string (possibly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{553 \textcolor{comment}{ * empty), never a NULL pointer, so it can be safely used in printf() and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{554 \textcolor{comment}{ * other string-\/handling functions.  Note that the "{}itxt\_length"{}, "{}lang"{}, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{555 \textcolor{comment}{ * "{}lang\_key"{} members of the structure only exist when the library is built}}
\DoxyCodeLine{556 \textcolor{comment}{ * with iTXt chunk support.  Prior to libpng-\/1.4.0 the library was built by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{557 \textcolor{comment}{ * default without iTXt support. Also note that when iTXt *is* supported,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{558 \textcolor{comment}{ * the "{}lang"{} and "{}lang\_key"{} fields contain NULL pointers when the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{559 \textcolor{comment}{ * "{}compression"{} field contains * PNG\_TEXT\_COMPRESSION\_NONE or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{560 \textcolor{comment}{ * PNG\_TEXT\_COMPRESSION\_zTXt. Note that the "{}compression value"{} is not the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{561 \textcolor{comment}{ * same as what appears in the PNG tEXt/zTXt/iTXt chunk's "{}compression flag"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{562 \textcolor{comment}{ * which is always 0 or 1, or its "{}compression method"{} which is always 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{563 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{789 \textcolor{comment}{/* The following callback receives png\_uint\_32 row\_number, int pass for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{790 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_bytep data of the row.  When transforming an interlaced image the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{791 \textcolor{comment}{ * row number is the row number within the sub-\/image of the interlace pass, so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{792 \textcolor{comment}{ * the value will increase to the height of the sub-\/image (not the full image)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{793 \textcolor{comment}{ * then reset to 0 for the next pass.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{794 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{795 \textcolor{comment}{ * Use PNG\_ROW\_FROM\_PASS\_ROW(row, pass) and PNG\_COL\_FROM\_PASS\_COL(col, pass) to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{796 \textcolor{comment}{ * find the output pixel (x,y) given an interlaced sub-\/image pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{797 \textcolor{comment}{ * (row,col,pass).  (See below for these macros.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{798 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{873 \textcolor{comment}{/* Section 4: exported functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{874 \textcolor{comment}{ * Here are the function definitions most commonly used.  This is not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{875 \textcolor{comment}{ * the place to find out how to use libpng.  See libpng-\/manual.txt for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{876 \textcolor{comment}{ * full explanation, see example.c for the summary.  This just provides}}
\DoxyCodeLine{877 \textcolor{comment}{ * a simple one line description of the use of each function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{878 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{879 \textcolor{comment}{ * The PNG\_EXPORT() and PNG\_EXPORTA() macros used below are defined in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{880 \textcolor{comment}{ * pngconf.h and in the *.dfn files in the scripts directory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{881 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{882 \textcolor{comment}{ *   PNG\_EXPORT(ordinal, type, name, (args));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{883 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{884 \textcolor{comment}{ *       ordinal:    ordinal that is used while building}}
\DoxyCodeLine{885 \textcolor{comment}{ *                   *.def files. The ordinal value is only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{886 \textcolor{comment}{ *                   relevant when preprocessing png.h with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{887 \textcolor{comment}{ *                   the *.dfn files for building symbol table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{888 \textcolor{comment}{ *                   entries, and are removed by pngconf.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{889 \textcolor{comment}{ *       type:       return type of the function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{890 \textcolor{comment}{ *       name:       function name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{891 \textcolor{comment}{ *       args:       function arguments, with types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{892 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{893 \textcolor{comment}{ * When we wish to append attributes to a function prototype we use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{894 \textcolor{comment}{ * the PNG\_EXPORTA() macro instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{895 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{896 \textcolor{comment}{ *   PNG\_EXPORTA(ordinal, type, name, (args), attributes);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{897 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{898 \textcolor{comment}{ *       ordinal, type, name, and args: same as in PNG\_EXPORT().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{899 \textcolor{comment}{ *       attributes: function attributes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{900 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{901 }
\DoxyCodeLine{902 \textcolor{comment}{/* Returns the version number of the library */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{903 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(1, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8c_adcf74eb8d1c01b3947355671db674353}{png\_access\_version\_number}}, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{904 }
\DoxyCodeLine{905 \textcolor{comment}{/* Tell lib we have already handled the first <num\_bytes> magic bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{906 \textcolor{comment}{ * Handling more than 8 bytes from the beginning of the file is an error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{907 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{908 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(2, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8c_ae7c48450c1fa17a7d3e3154883cf2249}{png\_set\_sig\_bytes}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num\_bytes));}
\DoxyCodeLine{909 }
\DoxyCodeLine{910 \textcolor{comment}{/* Check sig[start] through sig[start + num\_to\_check -\/ 1] to see if it's a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{911 \textcolor{comment}{ * PNG file.  Returns zero if the supplied bytes match the 8-\/byte PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{912 \textcolor{comment}{ * signature, and non-\/zero otherwise.  Having num\_to\_check == 0 or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{913 \textcolor{comment}{ * start > 7 will always fail (ie return non-\/zero).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{914 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{915 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(3, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8c_a54e9817412c05cfb88fa836a9f01edef}{png\_sig\_cmp}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a2e608af822427492832d11909c2f3fee}{png\_const\_bytep}} sig, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_adad3a3824fbe72fb0b01074bb01ebe75}{start}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{916     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} num\_to\_check));}
\DoxyCodeLine{917 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1095 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1096 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1097 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_READ\_ALPHA\_MODE\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1098 \textcolor{comment}{/* How the alpha channel is interpreted -\/ this affects how the color channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1099 \textcolor{comment}{ * of a PNG file are returned to the calling application when an alpha channel,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1100 \textcolor{comment}{ * or a tRNS chunk in a palette file, is present.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1101 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1102 \textcolor{comment}{ * This has no effect on the way pixels are written into a PNG output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1103 \textcolor{comment}{ * datastream. The color samples in a PNG datastream are never premultiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1104 \textcolor{comment}{ * with the alpha samples.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1105 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1106 \textcolor{comment}{ * The default is to return data according to the PNG specification: the alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1107 \textcolor{comment}{ * channel is a linear measure of the contribution of the pixel to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1108 \textcolor{comment}{ * corresponding composited pixel, and the color channels are unassociated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1109 \textcolor{comment}{ * (not premultiplied).  The gamma encoded color channels must be scaled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1110 \textcolor{comment}{ * according to the contribution and to do this it is necessary to undo}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1111 \textcolor{comment}{ * the encoding, scale the color values, perform the composition and re-\/encode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1112 \textcolor{comment}{ * the values.  This is the 'PNG' mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1113 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1114 \textcolor{comment}{ * The alternative is to 'associate' the alpha with the color information by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1115 \textcolor{comment}{ * storing color channel values that have been scaled by the alpha.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1116 \textcolor{comment}{ * image.  These are the 'STANDARD', 'ASSOCIATED' or 'PREMULTIPLIED' modes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1117 \textcolor{comment}{ * (the latter being the two common names for associated alpha color channels).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1118 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1119 \textcolor{comment}{ * For the 'OPTIMIZED' mode, a pixel is treated as opaque only if the alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1120 \textcolor{comment}{ * value is equal to the maximum value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1121 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1122 \textcolor{comment}{ * The final choice is to gamma encode the alpha channel as well.  This is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1123 \textcolor{comment}{ * broken because, in practice, no implementation that uses this choice}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1124 \textcolor{comment}{ * correctly undoes the encoding before handling alpha composition.  Use this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1125 \textcolor{comment}{ * choice only if other serious errors in the software or hardware you use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1126 \textcolor{comment}{ * mandate it; the typical serious error is for dark halos to appear around}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1127 \textcolor{comment}{ * opaque areas of the composited PNG image because of arithmetic overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1128 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1129 \textcolor{comment}{ * The API function png\_set\_alpha\_mode specifies which of these choices to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1130 \textcolor{comment}{ * with an enumerated 'mode' value and the gamma of the required output:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1131 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1132 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG           0 }\textcolor{comment}{/* according to the PNG standard */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1133 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ALPHA\_STANDARD      1 }\textcolor{comment}{/* according to Porter/Duff */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1134 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ALPHA\_ASSOCIATED    1 }\textcolor{comment}{/* as above; this is the normal practice */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1135 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ALPHA\_PREMULTIPLIED 1 }\textcolor{comment}{/* as above */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1136 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ALPHA\_OPTIMIZED     2 }\textcolor{comment}{/* 'PNG' for opaque pixels, else 'STANDARD' */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1137 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ALPHA\_BROKEN        3 }\textcolor{comment}{/* the alpha channel is gamma encoded */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1138 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1139 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a54fa41bbae77ea832e71fe471c6400a5}{PNG\_FP\_EXPORT}}(227, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngrtran_8c_ae049888ece85e1d291effc930a8e4621}{png\_set\_alpha\_mode}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a3eabae3e1e65723a7ec3445646cb7795}{mode}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{1140     \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} output\_gamma))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1141 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a767877e32606b8f089120c81e3a43155}{PNG\_FIXED\_EXPORT}}(228, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a2feda30cf8b3e63060e852d77a278728}{png\_set\_alpha\_mode\_fixed}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{1142     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a3eabae3e1e65723a7ec3445646cb7795}{mode}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a23911f489715bb4644c9c9c808cbab5a}{png\_fixed\_point}} output\_gamma))}
\DoxyCodeLine{1143 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1144 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1145 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(PNG\_GAMMA\_SUPPORTED) || defined(PNG\_READ\_ALPHA\_MODE\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1146 \textcolor{comment}{/* The output\_gamma value is a screen gamma in libpng terminology: it expresses}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1147 \textcolor{comment}{ * how to decode the output values, not how they are encoded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1148 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1149 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB -\/1       }\textcolor{comment}{/* sRGB gamma and color space */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1150 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_GAMMA\_MAC\_18 -\/2       }\textcolor{comment}{/* Old Mac '1.8' gamma and color space */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1151 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_GAMMA\_sRGB   220000   }\textcolor{comment}{/* Television standards-\/-\/matches sRGB gamma */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1152 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_GAMMA\_LINEAR PNG\_FP\_1 }\textcolor{comment}{/* Linear */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1153 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1154 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1155 \textcolor{comment}{/* The following are examples of calls to png\_set\_alpha\_mode to achieve the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1156 \textcolor{comment}{ * required overall gamma correction and, where necessary, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1157 \textcolor{comment}{ * premultiplication.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1158 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1159 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG, PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1160 \textcolor{comment}{ *    This is the default libpng handling of the alpha channel -\/ it is not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1161 \textcolor{comment}{ *    pre-\/multiplied into the color components.  In addition the call states}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1162 \textcolor{comment}{ *    that the output is for a sRGB system and causes all PNG files without gAMA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1163 \textcolor{comment}{ *    chunks to be assumed to be encoded using sRGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1164 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1165 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG, PNG\_GAMMA\_MAC);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1166 \textcolor{comment}{ *    In this case the output is assumed to be something like an sRGB conformant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1167 \textcolor{comment}{ *    display preceded by a power-\/law lookup table of power 1.45.  This is how}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1168 \textcolor{comment}{ *    early Mac systems behaved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1169 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1170 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_STANDARD, PNG\_GAMMA\_LINEAR);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1171 \textcolor{comment}{ *    This is the classic Jim Blinn approach and will work in academic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1172 \textcolor{comment}{ *    environments where everything is done by the book.  It has the shortcoming}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1173 \textcolor{comment}{ *    of assuming that input PNG data with no gamma information is linear -\/ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1174 \textcolor{comment}{ *    is unlikely to be correct unless the PNG files where generated locally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1175 \textcolor{comment}{ *    Most of the time the output precision will be so low as to show}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1176 \textcolor{comment}{ *    significant banding in dark areas of the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1177 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1178 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_expand\_16(pp);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1179 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_STANDARD, PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1180 \textcolor{comment}{ *    This is a somewhat more realistic Jim Blinn inspired approach.  PNG files}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1181 \textcolor{comment}{ *    are assumed to have the sRGB encoding if not marked with a gamma value and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1182 \textcolor{comment}{ *    the output is always 16 bits per component.  This permits accurate scaling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1183 \textcolor{comment}{ *    and processing of the data.  If you know that your input PNG files were}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1184 \textcolor{comment}{ *    generated locally you might need to replace PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1185 \textcolor{comment}{ *    correct value for your system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1186 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1187 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_OPTIMIZED, PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1188 \textcolor{comment}{ *    If you just need to composite the PNG image onto an existing background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1189 \textcolor{comment}{ *    and if you control the code that does this you can use the optimization}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1190 \textcolor{comment}{ *    setting.  In this case you just copy completely opaque pixels to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1191 \textcolor{comment}{ *    output.  For pixels that are not completely transparent (you just skip}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1192 \textcolor{comment}{ *    those) you do the composition math using png\_composite or png\_composite\_16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1193 \textcolor{comment}{ *    below then encode the resultant 8-\/bit or 16-\/bit values to match the output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1194 \textcolor{comment}{ *    encoding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1195 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1196 \textcolor{comment}{ * Other cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1197 \textcolor{comment}{ *    If neither the PNG nor the standard linear encoding work for you because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1198 \textcolor{comment}{ *    of the software or hardware you use then you have a big problem.  The PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1199 \textcolor{comment}{ *    case will probably result in halos around the image.  The linear encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1200 \textcolor{comment}{ *    will probably result in a washed out, too bright, image (it's actually too}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1201 \textcolor{comment}{ *    contrasty.)  Try the ALPHA\_OPTIMIZED mode above -\/ this will probably}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1202 \textcolor{comment}{ *    substantially reduce the halos.  Alternatively try:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1203 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1204 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_BROKEN, PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1205 \textcolor{comment}{ *    This option will also reduce the halos, but there will be slight dark}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1206 \textcolor{comment}{ *    halos round the opaque parts of the image where the background is light.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1207 \textcolor{comment}{ *    In the OPTIMIZED mode the halos will be light halos where the background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1208 \textcolor{comment}{ *    is dark.  Take your pick -\/ the halos are unavoidable unless you can get}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1209 \textcolor{comment}{ *    your hardware/software fixed!  (The OPTIMIZED approach is slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1210 \textcolor{comment}{ *    faster.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1211 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1212 \textcolor{comment}{ * When the default gamma of PNG files doesn't match the output gamma.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1213 \textcolor{comment}{ *    If you have PNG files with no gamma information png\_set\_alpha\_mode allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1214 \textcolor{comment}{ *    you to provide a default gamma, but it also sets the output gamma to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1215 \textcolor{comment}{ *    matching value.  If you know your PNG files have a gamma that doesn't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1216 \textcolor{comment}{ *    match the output you can take advantage of the fact that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1217 \textcolor{comment}{ *    png\_set\_alpha\_mode always sets the output gamma but only sets the PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1218 \textcolor{comment}{ *    default if it is not already set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1219 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1220 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG, PNG\_DEFAULT\_sRGB);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1221 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_set\_alpha\_mode(pp, PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG, PNG\_GAMMA\_MAC);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1222 \textcolor{comment}{ *    The first call sets both the default and the output gamma values, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1223 \textcolor{comment}{ *    second call overrides the output gamma without changing the default.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1224 \textcolor{comment}{ *    is easier than achieving the same effect with png\_set\_gamma.  You must use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1225 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG for the first call -\/ internal checking in png\_set\_alpha will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1226 \textcolor{comment}{ *    fire if more than one call to png\_set\_alpha\_mode and png\_set\_background is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1227 \textcolor{comment}{ *    made in the same read operation, however multiple calls with PNG\_ALPHA\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1228 \textcolor{comment}{ *    are ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1229 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1230 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1231 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_READ\_STRIP\_ALPHA\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1232 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(36, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngrtran_8c_a0a78aff372feaafce4bc15c19974e883}{png\_set\_strip\_alpha}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1233 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1234 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1235 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(PNG\_READ\_SWAP\_ALPHA\_SUPPORTED) || \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1236 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    defined(PNG\_WRITE\_SWAP\_ALPHA\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1237 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(37, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngtrans_8c_ae51012a5f024c0f93a8209860645c71d}{png\_set\_swap\_alpha}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1238 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1239 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1429 \textcolor{comment}{/* Values for png\_set\_crc\_action() say how to handle CRC errors in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1430 \textcolor{comment}{ * ancillary and critical chunks, and whether to use the data contained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1431 \textcolor{comment}{ * therein.  Note that it is impossible to "{}discard"{} data in a critical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1432 \textcolor{comment}{ * chunk.  For versions prior to 0.90, the action was always error/quit,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1433 \textcolor{comment}{ * whereas in version 0.90 and later, the action for CRC errors in ancillary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1434 \textcolor{comment}{ * chunks is warn/discard.  These values should NOT be changed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1435 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1436 \textcolor{comment}{ *      value                       action:critical     action:ancillary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1437 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1438 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CRC\_DEFAULT       0  }\textcolor{comment}{/* error/quit          warn/discard data */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1439 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CRC\_ERROR\_QUIT    1  }\textcolor{comment}{/* error/quit          error/quit        */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1440 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CRC\_WARN\_DISCARD  2  }\textcolor{comment}{/* (INVALID)           warn/discard data */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1441 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CRC\_WARN\_USE      3  }\textcolor{comment}{/* warn/use data       warn/use data     */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1442 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CRC\_QUIET\_USE     4  }\textcolor{comment}{/* quiet/use data      quiet/use data    */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1443 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CRC\_NO\_CHANGE     5  }\textcolor{comment}{/* use current value   use current value */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1444 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1649 \textcolor{comment}{/* This callback is called only for *unknown* chunks.  If}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1651 \textcolor{comment}{ * chunks to be treated as unknown, however in this case the callback must do}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1657 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1658 \textcolor{comment}{ * The integer return from the callback function is interpreted thus:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1659 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1660 \textcolor{comment}{ * negative: An error occurred; png\_chunk\_error will be called.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1661 \textcolor{comment}{ *     zero: The chunk was not handled, the chunk will be saved. A critical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1662 \textcolor{comment}{ *           chunk will cause an error at this point unless it is to be saved.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1701 \textcolor{comment}{/* A function which may be called *only* outside (after) a call to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1702 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_process\_data.  It returns the number of bytes of data to skip in the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1827 \textcolor{comment}{/* The png\_set\_<chunk> functions are for storing values in the png\_info\_struct.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1828 \textcolor{comment}{ * Similarly, the png\_get\_<chunk> calls are used to read values from the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1829 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_info\_struct, either storing the parameters in the passed variables, or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830 \textcolor{comment}{ * setting pointers into the png\_info\_struct where the data is stored.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1831 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_get\_<chunk> functions return a non-\/zero value if the data was available}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1832 \textcolor{comment}{ * in info\_ptr, or return zero and do not change any of the parameters if the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1833 \textcolor{comment}{ * data was not available.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1834 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835 \textcolor{comment}{ * These functions should be used instead of directly accessing png\_info}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836 \textcolor{comment}{ * to avoid problems with future changes in the size and internal layout of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1837 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_info\_struct.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2179 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* sCAL */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2180 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2181 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_SET\_UNKNOWN\_CHUNKS\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2182 \textcolor{comment}{/* Provide the default handling for all unknown chunks or, optionally, for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2183 \textcolor{comment}{ * specific unknown chunks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2184 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2185 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: prior to 1.6.0 the handling specified for particular chunks on read was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2186 \textcolor{comment}{ * ignored and the default was used, the per-\/chunk setting only had an effect on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2187 \textcolor{comment}{ * write.  If you wish to have chunk-\/specific handling on read in code that must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2188 \textcolor{comment}{ * work on earlier versions you must use a user chunk callback to specify the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2189 \textcolor{comment}{ * desired handling (keep or discard.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2190 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2191 \textcolor{comment}{ * The 'keep' parameter is a PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_ value as listed below.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2192 \textcolor{comment}{ * parameter is interpreted as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2193 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2194 \textcolor{comment}{ * READ:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2195 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_AS\_DEFAULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2196 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Known chunks: do normal libpng processing, do not keep the chunk (but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2197 \textcolor{comment}{ *          see the comments below about PNG\_HANDLE\_AS\_UNKNOWN\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2198 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Unknown chunks: for a specific chunk use the global default, when used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2199 \textcolor{comment}{ *          as the default discard the chunk data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2200 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_NEVER:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2201 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Discard the chunk data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2202 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2203 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Keep the chunk data if the chunk is not critical else raise a chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2204 \textcolor{comment}{ *       error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2205 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_ALWAYS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2206 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Keep the chunk data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2207 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2208 \textcolor{comment}{ * If the chunk data is saved it can be retrieved using png\_get\_unknown\_chunks,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2209 \textcolor{comment}{ * below.  Notice that specifying "{}AS\_DEFAULT"{} as a global default is equivalent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2210 \textcolor{comment}{ * to specifying "{}NEVER"{}, however when "{}AS\_DEFAULT"{} is used for specific chunks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2211 \textcolor{comment}{ * it simply resets the behavior to the libpng default.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2212 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2213 \textcolor{comment}{ * INTERACTION WITH USER CHUNK CALLBACKS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2214 \textcolor{comment}{ * The per-\/chunk handling is always used when there is a png\_user\_chunk\_ptr}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2215 \textcolor{comment}{ * callback and the callback returns 0; the chunk is then always stored *unless*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2216 \textcolor{comment}{ * it is critical and the per-\/chunk setting is other than ALWAYS.  Notice that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2217 \textcolor{comment}{ * the global default is *not* used in this case.  (In effect the per-\/chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2218 \textcolor{comment}{ * value is incremented to at least IF\_SAFE.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2219 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2220 \textcolor{comment}{ * IMPORTANT NOTE: this behavior will change in libpng 1.7 -\/ the global and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2221 \textcolor{comment}{ * per-\/chunk defaults will be honored.  If you want to preserve the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2222 \textcolor{comment}{ * behavior when your callback returns 0 you must set PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2223 \textcolor{comment}{ * as the default -\/ if you don't do this libpng 1.6 will issue a warning.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2224 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2225 \textcolor{comment}{ * If you want unhandled unknown chunks to be discarded in libpng 1.6 and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2226 \textcolor{comment}{ * earlier simply return '1' (handled).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2227 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2228 \textcolor{comment}{ * PNG\_HANDLE\_AS\_UNKNOWN\_SUPPORTED:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2229 \textcolor{comment}{ *    If this is *not* set known chunks will always be handled by libpng and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2230 \textcolor{comment}{ *    will never be stored in the unknown chunk list.  Known chunks listed to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2231 \textcolor{comment}{ *    png\_set\_keep\_unknown\_chunks will have no effect.  If it is set then known}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2232 \textcolor{comment}{ *    chunks listed with a keep other than AS\_DEFAULT will *never* be processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2233 \textcolor{comment}{ *    by libpng, in addition critical chunks must either be processed by the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2234 \textcolor{comment}{ *    callback or saved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2235 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2236 \textcolor{comment}{ *    The IHDR and IEND chunks must not be listed.  Because this turns off the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2237 \textcolor{comment}{ *    default handling for chunks that would otherwise be recognized the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2238 \textcolor{comment}{ *    behavior of libpng transformations may well become incorrect!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2239 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2240 \textcolor{comment}{ * WRITE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2241 \textcolor{comment}{ *    When writing chunks the options only apply to the chunks specified by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2242 \textcolor{comment}{ *    png\_set\_unknown\_chunks (below), libpng will *always* write known chunks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2243 \textcolor{comment}{ *    required by png\_set\_ calls and will always write the core critical chunks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2244 \textcolor{comment}{ *    (as required for PLTE).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2245 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2246 \textcolor{comment}{ *    Each chunk in the png\_set\_unknown\_chunks list is looked up in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2247 \textcolor{comment}{ *    png\_set\_keep\_unknown\_chunks list to find the keep setting, this is then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2248 \textcolor{comment}{ *    interpreted as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2249 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2250 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_AS\_DEFAULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2251 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Write safe-\/to-\/copy chunks and write other chunks if the global}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2252 \textcolor{comment}{ *       default is set to \_ALWAYS, otherwise don't write this chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2253 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_NEVER:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2254 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Do not write the chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2255 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2256 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Write the chunk if it is safe-\/to-\/copy, otherwise do not write it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2257 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_ALWAYS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2258 \textcolor{comment}{ *       Write the chunk.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2259 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2260 \textcolor{comment}{ * Note that the default behavior is effectively the opposite of the read case -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2261 \textcolor{comment}{ * in read unknown chunks are not stored by default, in write they are written}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2262 \textcolor{comment}{ * by default.  Also the behavior of PNG\_HANDLE\_CHUNK\_IF\_SAFE is very different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2263 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ on write the safe-\/to-\/copy bit is checked, on read the critical bit is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2264 \textcolor{comment}{ * checked and on read if the chunk is critical an error will be raised.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2265 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2266 \textcolor{comment}{ * num\_chunks:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2267 \textcolor{comment}{ * ===========}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2268 \textcolor{comment}{ *    If num\_chunks is positive, then the "{}keep"{} parameter specifies the manner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2269 \textcolor{comment}{ *    for handling only those chunks appearing in the chunk\_list array,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2270 \textcolor{comment}{ *    otherwise the chunk list array is ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2271 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2272 \textcolor{comment}{ *    If num\_chunks is 0 the "{}keep"{} parameter specifies the default behavior for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2273 \textcolor{comment}{ *    unknown chunks, as described above.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2274 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2275 \textcolor{comment}{ *    If num\_chunks is negative, then the "{}keep"{} parameter specifies the manner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2276 \textcolor{comment}{ *    for handling all unknown chunks plus all chunks recognized by libpng}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2277 \textcolor{comment}{ *    except for the IHDR, PLTE, tRNS, IDAT, and IEND chunks (which continue to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2278 \textcolor{comment}{ *    be processed by libpng.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2279 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2280 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_HANDLE\_AS\_UNKNOWN\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2281 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(172, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngset_8c_a341332fd115af9add2204c36a95a9a4e}{png\_set\_keep\_unknown\_chunks}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_afd0519b307fc9e36f645ad6eaf620d05}{png\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{2282     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} keep, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a2e608af822427492832d11909c2f3fee}{png\_const\_bytep}} chunk\_list, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num\_chunks));}

\DoxyCodeLine{2422 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2423 \textcolor{comment}{/* The flags returned by png\_get\_io\_state() are the following: */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2424 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_NONE        0x0000   }\textcolor{comment}{/* no I/O at this moment */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2425 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_READING     0x0001   }\textcolor{comment}{/* currently reading */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2426 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_WRITING     0x0002   }\textcolor{comment}{/* currently writing */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2427 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_SIGNATURE   0x0010   }\textcolor{comment}{/* currently at the file signature */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2428 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_CHUNK\_HDR   0x0020   }\textcolor{comment}{/* currently at the chunk header */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2429 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_CHUNK\_DATA  0x0040   }\textcolor{comment}{/* currently at the chunk data */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2430 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_CHUNK\_CRC   0x0080   }\textcolor{comment}{/* currently at the chunk crc */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2431 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_MASK\_OP     0x000f   }\textcolor{comment}{/* current operation: reading/writing */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2432 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IO\_MASK\_LOC    0x00f0   }\textcolor{comment}{/* current location: sig/hdr/data/crc */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2433 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* IO\_STATE */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2434 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2435 \textcolor{comment}{/* Interlace support.  The following macros are always defined so that if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436 \textcolor{comment}{ * libpng interlace handling is turned off the macros may be used to handle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2437 \textcolor{comment}{ * interlaced images within the application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2439 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_INTERLACE\_ADAM7\_PASSES 7}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2441 \textcolor{comment}{/* Two macros to return the first row and first column of the original,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442 \textcolor{comment}{ * full, image which appears in a given pass.  'pass' is in the range 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443 \textcolor{comment}{ * to 6 and the result is in the range 0 to 7.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2444 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2445 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_START\_ROW(pass) (((1\&\string~(pass))<<(3-\/((pass)>>1)))\&7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2446 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_START\_COL(pass) (((1\& (pass))<<(3-\/(((pass)+1)>>1)))\&7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2447 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2448 \textcolor{comment}{/* A macro to return the offset between pixels in the output row for a pair of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2449 \textcolor{comment}{ * pixels in the input -\/ effectively the inverse of the 'COL\_SHIFT' macro that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2450 \textcolor{comment}{ * follows.  Note that ROW\_OFFSET is the offset from one row to the next whereas}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2451 \textcolor{comment}{ * COL\_OFFSET is from one column to the next, within a row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2452 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2453 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_OFFSET(pass) ((pass)>2?(8>>(((pass)-\/1)>>1)):8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2454 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_COL\_OFFSET(pass) (1<<((7-\/(pass))>>1))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2455 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2456 \textcolor{comment}{/* Two macros to help evaluate the number of rows or columns in each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2457 \textcolor{comment}{ * pass.  This is expressed as a shift -\/ effectively log2 of the number or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2458 \textcolor{comment}{ * rows or columns in each 8x8 tile of the original image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2459 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2460 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_SHIFT(pass) ((pass)>2?(8-\/(pass))>>1:3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2461 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_COL\_SHIFT(pass) ((pass)>1?(7-\/(pass))>>1:3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2462 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2463 \textcolor{comment}{/* Hence two macros to determine the number of rows or columns in a given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2464 \textcolor{comment}{ * pass of an image given its height or width.  In fact these macros may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2465 \textcolor{comment}{ * return non-\/zero even though the sub-\/image is empty, because the other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2466 \textcolor{comment}{ * dimension may be empty for a small image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2467 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2468 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_ROWS(height, pass) (((height)+(((1<<PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_SHIFT(pass))\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2469 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   -\/1)-\/PNG\_PASS\_START\_ROW(pass)))>>PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_SHIFT(pass))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2470 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_COLS(width, pass) (((width)+(((1<<PNG\_PASS\_COL\_SHIFT(pass))\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2471 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   -\/1)-\/PNG\_PASS\_START\_COL(pass)))>>PNG\_PASS\_COL\_SHIFT(pass))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2472 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2473 \textcolor{comment}{/* For the reader row callbacks (both progressive and sequential) it is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2474 \textcolor{comment}{ * necessary to find the row in the output image given a row in an interlaced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2475 \textcolor{comment}{ * image, so two more macros:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2476 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2477 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ROW\_FROM\_PASS\_ROW(y\_in, pass) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2478 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (((y\_in)<<PNG\_PASS\_ROW\_SHIFT(pass))+PNG\_PASS\_START\_ROW(pass))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2479 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_COL\_FROM\_PASS\_COL(x\_in, pass) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2480 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (((x\_in)<<PNG\_PASS\_COL\_SHIFT(pass))+PNG\_PASS\_START\_COL(pass))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2481 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2482 \textcolor{comment}{/* Two macros which return a boolean (0 or 1) saying whether the given row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2483 \textcolor{comment}{ * or column is in a particular pass.  These use a common utility macro that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2484 \textcolor{comment}{ * returns a mask for a given pass -\/ the offset 'off' selects the row or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2485 \textcolor{comment}{ * column version.  The mask has the appropriate bit set for each column in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2486 \textcolor{comment}{ * the tile.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2487 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2488 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PASS\_MASK(pass,off) ( \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2489 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((0x110145AF>>(((7-\/(off))-\/(pass))<<2)) \& 0xF) | \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2490 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((0x01145AF0>>(((7-\/(off))-\/(pass))<<2)) \& 0xF0))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2491 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2492 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ROW\_IN\_INTERLACE\_PASS(y, pass) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2493 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((PNG\_PASS\_MASK(pass,0) >> ((y)\&7)) \& 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2494 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_COL\_IN\_INTERLACE\_PASS(x, pass) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2495 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((PNG\_PASS\_MASK(pass,1) >> ((x)\&7)) \& 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2496 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2497 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_READ\_COMPOSITE\_NODIV\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2498 \textcolor{comment}{/* With these routines we avoid an integer divide, which will be slower on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2499 \textcolor{comment}{ * most machines.  However, it does take more operations than the corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2500 \textcolor{comment}{ * divide method, so it may be slower on a few RISC systems.  There are two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2501 \textcolor{comment}{ * shifts (by 8 or 16 bits) and an addition, versus a single integer divide.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2502 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2503 \textcolor{comment}{ * Note that the rounding factors are NOT supposed to be the same!  128 and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2504 \textcolor{comment}{ * 32768 are correct for the NODIV code; 127 and 32767 are correct for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2505 \textcolor{comment}{ * standard method.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2506 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2507 \textcolor{comment}{ * [Optimized code by Greg Roelofs and Mark Adler...blame us for bugs. :-\/) ]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2508 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2509 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2510  \textcolor{comment}{/* fg and bg should be in `gamma 1.0' space; alpha is the opacity */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2511 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2512 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_composite(composite, fg, alpha, bg)        \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2513 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \{                                                     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2514 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      png\_uint\_16 temp = (png\_uint\_16)((png\_uint\_16)(fg) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2515 \textcolor{preprocessor}{          * (png\_uint\_16)(alpha)                         \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2516 \textcolor{preprocessor}{          + (png\_uint\_16)(bg)*(png\_uint\_16)(255          \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2517 \textcolor{preprocessor}{          -\/ (png\_uint\_16)(alpha)) + 128);                \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2518 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      (composite) = (png\_byte)(((temp + (temp >> 8)) >> 8) \& 0xff); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2519 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2520 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2521 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_composite\_16(composite, fg, alpha, bg)     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2522 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \{                                                     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2523 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      png\_uint\_32 temp = (png\_uint\_32)((png\_uint\_32)(fg) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2524 \textcolor{preprocessor}{          * (png\_uint\_32)(alpha)                         \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2525 \textcolor{preprocessor}{          + (png\_uint\_32)(bg)*(65535                     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2526 \textcolor{preprocessor}{          -\/ (png\_uint\_32)(alpha)) + 32768);              \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2527 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      (composite) = (png\_uint\_16)(0xffff \& ((temp + (temp >> 16)) >> 16)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2528 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2529 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2530 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Standard method using integer division */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2531 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2532 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_composite(composite, fg, alpha, bg)                      \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2533 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (composite) =                                                       \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2534 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       (png\_byte)(0xff \& (((png\_uint\_16)(fg) * (png\_uint\_16)(alpha) +  \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2535 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       (png\_uint\_16)(bg) * (png\_uint\_16)(255 -\/ (png\_uint\_16)(alpha)) + \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2536 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       127) / 255))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2537 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2538 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_composite\_16(composite, fg, alpha, bg)                       \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2539 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (composite) =                                                           \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2540 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       (png\_uint\_16)(0xffff \& (((png\_uint\_32)(fg) * (png\_uint\_32)(alpha) + \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2541 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       (png\_uint\_32)(bg)*(png\_uint\_32)(65535 -\/ (png\_uint\_32)(alpha)) +     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2542 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       32767) / 65535))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2543 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* READ\_COMPOSITE\_NODIV */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2544 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2545 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_READ\_INT\_FUNCTIONS\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2546 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(201, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aacdd3ade0dd6cf6ae78ad2460eba2dfc}{png\_get\_uint\_32}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a2e608af822427492832d11909c2f3fee}{png\_const\_bytep}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_ab998012e627da2312fc60f51c0c2f313}{buf}}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2547 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(202, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngrutil_8c_a7b67546e4211b127dd370e8ef197bc3f}{png\_uint\_16}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a02a6a840b3153210862859baf0e92e52}{png\_get\_uint\_16}}, (\mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a2e608af822427492832d11909c2f3fee}{png\_const\_bytep}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_ab998012e627da2312fc60f51c0c2f313}{buf}}));}

\DoxyCodeLine{2572 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_USE\_READ\_MACROS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2573 \textcolor{comment}{/* Inline macros to do direct reads of bytes from the input buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2574 \textcolor{comment}{ * The png\_get\_int\_32() routine assumes we are using two's complement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2575 \textcolor{comment}{ * format for negative values, which is almost certainly true.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2576 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2577 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_get\_uint\_32(buf) \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2579 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((png\_uint\_32)(*((buf) + 1)) << 16) + \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2580 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((png\_uint\_32)(*((buf) + 2)) << 8) + \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2581 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((png\_uint\_32)(*((buf) + 3))))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2582 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2583    \textcolor{comment}{/* From libpng-\/1.4.0 until 1.4.4, the png\_get\_uint\_16 macro (but not the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2584 \textcolor{comment}{    * function) incorrectly returned a value of type png\_uint\_32.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2585 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2586 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_get\_uint\_16(buf) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2587 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((png\_uint\_16) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2588 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    (((unsigned int)(*(buf)) << 8) + \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2589 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((unsigned int)(*((buf) + 1)))))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2590 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2591 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_get\_int\_32(buf) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2592 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((png\_int\_32)((*(buf) \& 0x80) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2593 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ? -\/((png\_int\_32)(((png\_get\_uint\_32(buf)\string^0xffffffffU)+1U)\&0x7fffffffU)) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2594 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    : (png\_int\_32)png\_get\_uint\_32(buf)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2595 }
