\DoxyCodeLine{2621 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2622 \textcolor{comment}{/*******************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2623 \textcolor{comment}{ * Section 5: SIMPLIFIED API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2624 \textcolor{comment}{ *******************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2625 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2626 \textcolor{comment}{ * Please read the documentation in libpng-\/manual.txt (TODO: write said}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2627 \textcolor{comment}{ * documentation) if you don't understand what follows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2628 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2629 \textcolor{comment}{ * The simplified API hides the details of both libpng and the PNG file format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2630 \textcolor{comment}{ * itself.  It allows PNG files to be read into a very limited number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2631 \textcolor{comment}{ * in-\/memory bitmap formats or to be written from the same formats.  If these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2632 \textcolor{comment}{ * formats do not accommodate your needs then you can, and should, use the more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2633 \textcolor{comment}{ * sophisticated APIs above -\/ these support a wide variety of in-\/memory formats}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2634 \textcolor{comment}{ * and a wide variety of sophisticated transformations to those formats as well}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2635 \textcolor{comment}{ * as a wide variety of APIs to manipulate ancillary information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2636 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2637 \textcolor{comment}{ * To read a PNG file using the simplified API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2638 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2639 \textcolor{comment}{ * 1) Declare a 'png\_image' structure (see below) on the stack, set the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2640 \textcolor{comment}{ *    version field to PNG\_IMAGE\_VERSION and the 'opaque' pointer to NULL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2641 \textcolor{comment}{ *    (this is REQUIRED, your program may crash if you don't do it.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2642 \textcolor{comment}{ * 2) Call the appropriate png\_image\_begin\_read... function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2643 \textcolor{comment}{ * 3) Set the png\_image 'format' member to the required sample format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2644 \textcolor{comment}{ * 4) Allocate a buffer for the image and, if required, the color-\/map.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2645 \textcolor{comment}{ * 5) Call png\_image\_finish\_read to read the image and, if required, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2646 \textcolor{comment}{ *    color-\/map into your buffers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2647 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2648 \textcolor{comment}{ * There are no restrictions on the format of the PNG input itself; all valid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2649 \textcolor{comment}{ * color types, bit depths, and interlace methods are acceptable, and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2650 \textcolor{comment}{ * input image is transformed as necessary to the requested in-\/memory format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2651 \textcolor{comment}{ * during the png\_image\_finish\_read() step.  The only caveat is that if you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2652 \textcolor{comment}{ * request a color-\/mapped image from a PNG that is full-\/color or makes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2653 \textcolor{comment}{ * complex use of an alpha channel the transformation is extremely lossy and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654 \textcolor{comment}{ * result may look terrible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656 \textcolor{comment}{ * To write a PNG file using the simplified API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2658 \textcolor{comment}{ * 1) Declare a 'png\_image' structure on the stack and memset() it to all zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2659 \textcolor{comment}{ * 2) Initialize the members of the structure that describe the image, setting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2660 \textcolor{comment}{ *    the 'format' member to the format of the image samples.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2661 \textcolor{comment}{ * 3) Call the appropriate png\_image\_write... function with a pointer to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2662 \textcolor{comment}{ *    image and, if necessary, the color-\/map to write the PNG data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2663 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2664 \textcolor{comment}{ * png\_image is a structure that describes the in-\/memory format of an image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2665 \textcolor{comment}{ * when it is being read or defines the in-\/memory format of an image that you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2666 \textcolor{comment}{ * need to write:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2667 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2668 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_READ\_SUPPORTED) || \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2669 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    defined(PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_WRITE\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2670 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2671 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_VERSION 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2672 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2673 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }png\_control *png\_controlp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2674 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2675 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2676    png\_controlp opaque;    \textcolor{comment}{/* Initialize to NULL, free with png\_image\_free */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2677    \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}  \mbox{\hyperlink{jpeglib_8h_aad880fc4455c253781e8968f2239d56f}{version}};   \textcolor{comment}{/* Set to PNG\_IMAGE\_VERSION */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2678    \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}  \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_ad46179dbe9c68fdcea52b34c3480ec0f}{width}};     \textcolor{comment}{/* Image width in pixels (columns) */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2679    \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}  \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_a33074d1196a1300c7cee5c0e42fa5cf8}{height}};    \textcolor{comment}{/* Image height in pixels (rows) */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2680    \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}  \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_a597b77c61fc6d444d2bfc6bf69dee277}{format}};    \textcolor{comment}{/* Image format as defined below */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2681    \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}  \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacejuce_a848bbbcf606d6a8175b2c2712055d209}{flags}};     \textcolor{comment}{/* A bit mask containing informational flags */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2682    \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}  colormap\_entries;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2683                            \textcolor{comment}{/* Number of entries in the color-\/map */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2685    \textcolor{comment}{/* In the event of an error or warning the following field will be set to a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2686 \textcolor{comment}{    * non-\/zero value and the 'message' field will contain a '\(\backslash\)0' terminated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2687 \textcolor{comment}{    * string with the libpng error or warning message.  If both warnings and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2688 \textcolor{comment}{    * an error were encountered, only the error is recorded.  If there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2689 \textcolor{comment}{    * are multiple warnings, only the first one is recorded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2690 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691 \textcolor{comment}{    * The upper 30 bits of this value are reserved, the low two bits contain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2692 \textcolor{comment}{    * a value as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2693 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2694 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IMAGE\_WARNING 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2695 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IMAGE\_ERROR 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2696    \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2697 \textcolor{comment}{    * The result is a two-\/bit code such that a value more than 1 indicates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2698 \textcolor{comment}{    * a failure in the API just called:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2699 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2700 \textcolor{comment}{    *    0 -\/ no warning or error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2701 \textcolor{comment}{    *    1 -\/ warning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2702 \textcolor{comment}{    *    2 -\/ error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2703 \textcolor{comment}{    *    3 -\/ error preceded by warning}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2704 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2705 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_IMAGE\_FAILED(png\_cntrl) ((((png\_cntrl).warning\_or\_error)\&0x03)>1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2706 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2707    \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aed373ad2e16fd6df7ccfa96329441d0d}{png\_uint\_32}}  warning\_or\_error;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2708 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2709    \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}         \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_a1243e1c99f08a099c7a70cc1a258034a}{message}}[64];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2710 \} png\_image, *png\_imagep;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2711 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2712 \textcolor{comment}{/* The samples of the image have one to four channels whose components have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2713 \textcolor{comment}{ * original values in the range 0 to 1.0:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2714 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2715 \textcolor{comment}{ * 1: A single gray or luminance channel (G).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2716 \textcolor{comment}{ * 2: A gray/luminance channel and an alpha channel (GA).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2717 \textcolor{comment}{ * 3: Three red, green, blue color channels (RGB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718 \textcolor{comment}{ * 4: Three color channels and an alpha channel (RGBA).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2719 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720 \textcolor{comment}{ * The components are encoded in one of two ways:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2722 \textcolor{comment}{ * a) As a small integer, value 0..255, contained in a single byte.  For the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2723 \textcolor{comment}{ * alpha channel the original value is simply value/255.  For the color or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2724 \textcolor{comment}{ * luminance channels the value is encoded according to the sRGB specification}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2725 \textcolor{comment}{ * and matches the 8-\/bit format expected by typical display devices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2726 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2727 \textcolor{comment}{ * The color/gray channels are not scaled (pre-\/multiplied) by the alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728 \textcolor{comment}{ * channel and are suitable for passing to color management software.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2729 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730 \textcolor{comment}{ * b) As a value in the range 0..65535, contained in a 2-\/byte integer.  All}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731 \textcolor{comment}{ * channels can be converted to the original value by dividing by 65535; all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2732 \textcolor{comment}{ * channels are linear.  Color channels use the RGB encoding (RGB end-\/points) of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2733 \textcolor{comment}{ * the sRGB specification.  This encoding is identified by the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2734 \textcolor{comment}{ * PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR flag below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2735 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2736 \textcolor{comment}{ * When the simplified API needs to convert between sRGB and linear colorspaces,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2737 \textcolor{comment}{ * the actual sRGB transfer curve defined in the sRGB specification (see the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2738 \textcolor{comment}{ * article at <https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SRGB>) is used, not the gamma=1/2.2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2739 \textcolor{comment}{ * approximation used elsewhere in libpng.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2740 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2741 \textcolor{comment}{ * When an alpha channel is present it is expected to denote pixel coverage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2742 \textcolor{comment}{ * of the color or luminance channels and is returned as an associated alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2743 \textcolor{comment}{ * channel: the color/gray channels are scaled (pre-\/multiplied) by the alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2744 \textcolor{comment}{ * value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2745 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2746 \textcolor{comment}{ * The samples are either contained directly in the image data, between 1 and 8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2747 \textcolor{comment}{ * bytes per pixel according to the encoding, or are held in a color-\/map indexed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2748 \textcolor{comment}{ * by bytes in the image data.  In the case of a color-\/map the color-\/map entries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2749 \textcolor{comment}{ * are individual samples, encoded as above, and the image data has one byte per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2750 \textcolor{comment}{ * pixel to select the relevant sample from the color-\/map.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2751 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2752 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2753 \textcolor{comment}{/* PNG\_FORMAT\_*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2754 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2755 \textcolor{comment}{ * \#defines to be used in png\_image::format.  Each \#define identifies a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2756 \textcolor{comment}{ * particular layout of sample data and, if present, alpha values.  There are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2757 \textcolor{comment}{ * separate defines for each of the two component encodings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2758 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2759 \textcolor{comment}{ * A format is built up using single bit flag values.  All combinations are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2760 \textcolor{comment}{ * valid.  Formats can be built up from the flag values or you can use one of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2761 \textcolor{comment}{ * the predefined values below.  When testing formats always use the FORMAT\_FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2762 \textcolor{comment}{ * macros to test for individual features -\/ future versions of the library may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2763 \textcolor{comment}{ * add new flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2764 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2765 \textcolor{comment}{ * When reading or writing color-\/mapped images the format should be set to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2766 \textcolor{comment}{ * format of the entries in the color-\/map then png\_image\_\{read,write\}\_colormap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2767 \textcolor{comment}{ * called to read or write the color-\/map and set the format correctly for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2768 \textcolor{comment}{ * image data.  Do not set the PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP bit directly!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2769 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2770 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: libpng can be built with particular features disabled. If you see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2771 \textcolor{comment}{ * compiler errors because the definition of one of the following flags has been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2772 \textcolor{comment}{ * compiled out it is because libpng does not have the required support.  It is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2773 \textcolor{comment}{ * possible, however, for the libpng configuration to enable the format on just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2774 \textcolor{comment}{ * read or just write; in that case you may see an error at run time.  You can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2775 \textcolor{comment}{ * guard against this by checking for the definition of the appropriate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2776 \textcolor{comment}{ * "{}\_SUPPORTED"{} macro, one of:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2777 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2778 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_\{READ,WRITE\}\_\{BGR,AFIRST\}\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2779 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2780 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA    0x01U }\textcolor{comment}{/* format with an alpha channel */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2781 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR    0x02U }\textcolor{comment}{/* color format: otherwise grayscale */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2782 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR   0x04U }\textcolor{comment}{/* 2-\/byte channels else 1-\/byte */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2783 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP 0x08U }\textcolor{comment}{/* image data is color-\/mapped */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2784 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2785 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2786 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_BGR    0x10U }\textcolor{comment}{/* BGR colors, else order is RGB */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2787 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2788 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2789 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_FORMAT\_AFIRST\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2790 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_AFIRST 0x20U }\textcolor{comment}{/* alpha channel comes first */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2791 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2792 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2793 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ASSOCIATED\_ALPHA 0x40U }\textcolor{comment}{/* alpha channel is associated */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2794 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2795 \textcolor{comment}{/* Commonly used formats have predefined macros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2796 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2797 \textcolor{comment}{ * First the single byte (sRGB) formats:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2798 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2799 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_GRAY 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2800 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_GA   PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2801 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_AG   (PNG\_FORMAT\_GA|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_AFIRST)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2802 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_RGB  PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2803 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR  (PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_BGR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2804 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_RGBA (PNG\_FORMAT\_RGB|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2805 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_ARGB (PNG\_FORMAT\_RGBA|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_AFIRST)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2806 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_BGRA (PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2807 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_ABGR (PNG\_FORMAT\_BGRA|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_AFIRST)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2808 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2809 \textcolor{comment}{/* Then the linear 2-\/byte formats.  When naming these "{}Y"{} is used to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2810 \textcolor{comment}{ * indicate a luminance (gray) channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2811 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2812 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_LINEAR\_Y PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2813 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_LINEAR\_Y\_ALPHA (PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2814 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_LINEAR\_RGB (PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2815 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_LINEAR\_RGB\_ALPHA \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2816 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2817 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2818 \textcolor{comment}{/* With color-\/mapped formats the image data is one byte for each pixel, the byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2819 \textcolor{comment}{ * is an index into the color-\/map which is formatted as above.  To obtain a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2820 \textcolor{comment}{ * color-\/mapped format it is sufficient just to add the PNG\_FOMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2821 \textcolor{comment}{ * to one of the above definitions, or you can use one of the definitions below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2822 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2823 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_RGB\_COLORMAP  (PNG\_FORMAT\_RGB|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2824 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR\_COLORMAP  (PNG\_FORMAT\_BGR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2825 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_RGBA\_COLORMAP (PNG\_FORMAT\_RGBA|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2826 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_ARGB\_COLORMAP (PNG\_FORMAT\_ARGB|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2827 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_BGRA\_COLORMAP (PNG\_FORMAT\_BGRA|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2828 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FORMAT\_ABGR\_COLORMAP (PNG\_FORMAT\_ABGR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2829 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2830 \textcolor{comment}{/* PNG\_IMAGE macros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2831 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2832 \textcolor{comment}{ * These are convenience macros to derive information from a png\_image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2833 \textcolor{comment}{ * structure.  The PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_ macros return values appropriate to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2834 \textcolor{comment}{ * actual image sample values -\/ either the entries in the color-\/map or the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2835 \textcolor{comment}{ * pixels in the image.  The PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_ macros return corresponding values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2836 \textcolor{comment}{ * for the pixels and will always return 1 for color-\/mapped formats.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2837 \textcolor{comment}{ * remaining macros return information about the rows in the image and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2838 \textcolor{comment}{ * complete image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2839 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2840 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: All the macros that take a png\_image::format parameter are compile time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2841 \textcolor{comment}{ * constants if the format parameter is, itself, a constant.  Therefore these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2842 \textcolor{comment}{ * macros can be used in array declarations and case labels where required.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2843 \textcolor{comment}{ * Similarly the macros are also pre-\/processor constants (sizeof is not used) so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2844 \textcolor{comment}{ * they can be used in \#if tests.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2845 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2846 \textcolor{comment}{ * First the information about the samples.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2847 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2848 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_CHANNELS(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2849 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (((fmt)\&(PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLOR|PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA))+1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2850    \textcolor{comment}{/* Return the total number of channels in a given format: 1..4 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2851 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2852 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_COMPONENT\_SIZE(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2853 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((((fmt) \& PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR) >> 2)+1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2854    \textcolor{comment}{/* Return the size in bytes of a single component of a pixel or color-\/map}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2855 \textcolor{comment}{    * entry (as appropriate) in the image: 1 or 2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2856 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2857 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2858 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_SIZE(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2859 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_CHANNELS(fmt) * PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_COMPONENT\_SIZE(fmt))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2860    \textcolor{comment}{/* This is the size of the sample data for one sample.  If the image is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2861 \textcolor{comment}{    * color-\/mapped it is the size of one color-\/map entry (and image pixels are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2862 \textcolor{comment}{    * one byte in size), otherwise it is the size of one image pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2863 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2864 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2865 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_MAXIMUM\_COLORMAP\_COMPONENTS(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2866 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_CHANNELS(fmt) * 256)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2867    \textcolor{comment}{/* The maximum size of the color-\/map required by the format expressed in a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2868 \textcolor{comment}{    * count of components.  This can be used to compile-\/time allocate a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2869 \textcolor{comment}{    * color-\/map:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2870 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2871 \textcolor{comment}{    * png\_uint\_16 colormap[PNG\_IMAGE\_MAXIMUM\_COLORMAP\_COMPONENTS(linear\_fmt)];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2872 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2873 \textcolor{comment}{    * png\_byte colormap[PNG\_IMAGE\_MAXIMUM\_COLORMAP\_COMPONENTS(sRGB\_fmt)];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2874 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2875 \textcolor{comment}{    * Alternatively use the PNG\_IMAGE\_COLORMAP\_SIZE macro below to use the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2876 \textcolor{comment}{    * information from one of the png\_image\_begin\_read\_ APIs and dynamically}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2877 \textcolor{comment}{    * allocate the required memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2878 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2879 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2880 \textcolor{comment}{/* Corresponding information about the pixels */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2881 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_(test,fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (((fmt)\&PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)?1:test(fmt))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2883 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2884 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_CHANNELS(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2885 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_(PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_CHANNELS,fmt)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2886    \textcolor{comment}{/* The number of separate channels (components) in a pixel; 1 for a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2887 \textcolor{comment}{    * color-\/mapped image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2888 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2889 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2890 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_COMPONENT\_SIZE(fmt)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_(PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_COMPONENT\_SIZE,fmt)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2892    \textcolor{comment}{/* The size, in bytes, of each component in a pixel; 1 for a color-\/mapped}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893 \textcolor{comment}{    * image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2894 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2895 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2896 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_SIZE(fmt) PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_(PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_SIZE,fmt)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897    \textcolor{comment}{/* The size, in bytes, of a complete pixel; 1 for a color-\/mapped image. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2898 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2899 \textcolor{comment}{/* Information about the whole row, or whole image */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2900 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_ROW\_STRIDE(image)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2901 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_CHANNELS((image).format) * (image).width)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2902    \textcolor{comment}{/* Return the total number of components in a single row of the image; this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2903 \textcolor{comment}{    * is the minimum 'row stride', the minimum count of components between each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2904 \textcolor{comment}{    * row.  For a color-\/mapped image this is the minimum number of bytes in a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2905 \textcolor{comment}{    * row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2906 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907 \textcolor{comment}{    * WARNING: this macro overflows for some images with more than one component}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908 \textcolor{comment}{    * and very large image widths.  libpng will refuse to process an image where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2909 \textcolor{comment}{    * this macro would overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2910 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2912 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_BUFFER\_SIZE(image, row\_stride)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (PNG\_IMAGE\_PIXEL\_COMPONENT\_SIZE((image).format)*(image).height*(row\_stride))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914    \textcolor{comment}{/* Return the size, in bytes, of an image buffer given a png\_image and a row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915 \textcolor{comment}{    * stride -\/ the number of components to leave space for in each row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917 \textcolor{comment}{    * WARNING: this macro overflows a 32-\/bit integer for some large PNG images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2918 \textcolor{comment}{    * libpng will refuse to process an image where such an overflow would occur.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2921 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_SIZE(image)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2922 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   PNG\_IMAGE\_BUFFER\_SIZE(image, PNG\_IMAGE\_ROW\_STRIDE(image))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2923    \textcolor{comment}{/* Return the size, in bytes, of the image in memory given just a png\_image;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2924 \textcolor{comment}{    * the row stride is the minimum stride required for the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2925 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2926 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2927 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_COLORMAP\_SIZE(image)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2928 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (PNG\_IMAGE\_SAMPLE\_SIZE((image).format) * (image).colormap\_entries)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2929    \textcolor{comment}{/* Return the size, in bytes, of the color-\/map of this image.  If the image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2930 \textcolor{comment}{    * format is not a color-\/map format this will return a size sufficient for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2931 \textcolor{comment}{    * 256 entries in the given format; check PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2932 \textcolor{comment}{    * you don't want to allocate a color-\/map in this case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2933 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2934 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2935 \textcolor{comment}{/* PNG\_IMAGE\_FLAG\_*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2936 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2937 \textcolor{comment}{ * Flags containing additional information about the image are held in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2938 \textcolor{comment}{ * 'flags' field of png\_image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2939 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2940 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_FLAG\_COLORSPACE\_NOT\_sRGB 0x01}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2941    \textcolor{comment}{/* This indicates that the RGB values of the in-\/memory bitmap do not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2942 \textcolor{comment}{    * correspond to the red, green and blue end-\/points defined by sRGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2943 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2944 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2945 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_FLAG\_FAST 0x02}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2946    \textcolor{comment}{/* On write emphasise speed over compression; the resultant PNG file will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2947 \textcolor{comment}{    * larger but will be produced significantly faster, particular for large}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2948 \textcolor{comment}{    * images.  Do not use this option for images which will be distributed, only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2949 \textcolor{comment}{    * used it when producing intermediate files that will be read back in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2950 \textcolor{comment}{    * repeatedly.  For a typical 24-\/bit image the option will double the read}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2951 \textcolor{comment}{    * speed at the cost of increasing the image size by 25\%, however for many}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2952 \textcolor{comment}{    * more compressible images the PNG file can be 10 times larger with only a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2953 \textcolor{comment}{    * slight speed gain.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2954 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2956 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_FLAG\_16BIT\_sRGB 0x04}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2957    \textcolor{comment}{/* On read if the image is a 16-\/bit per component image and there is no gAMA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2958 \textcolor{comment}{    * or sRGB chunk assume that the components are sRGB encoded.  Notice that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2959 \textcolor{comment}{    * images output by the simplified API always have gamma information; setting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2960 \textcolor{comment}{    * this flag only affects the interpretation of 16-\/bit images from an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2961 \textcolor{comment}{    * external source.  It is recommended that the application expose this flag}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2962 \textcolor{comment}{    * to the user; the user can normally easily recognize the difference between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2963 \textcolor{comment}{    * linear and sRGB encoding.  This flag has no effect on write -\/ the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2964 \textcolor{comment}{    * passed to the write APIs must have the correct encoding (as defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2965 \textcolor{comment}{    * above.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2966 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2967 \textcolor{comment}{    * If the flag is not set (the default) input 16-\/bit per component data is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2968 \textcolor{comment}{    * assumed to be linear.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2969 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2970 \textcolor{comment}{    * NOTE: the flag can only be set after the png\_image\_begin\_read\_ call,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2971 \textcolor{comment}{    * because that call initializes the 'flags' field.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2972 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2973 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2974 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_READ\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2975 \textcolor{comment}{/* READ APIs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2976 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2977 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2978 \textcolor{comment}{ * The png\_image passed to the read APIs must have been initialized by setting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2979 \textcolor{comment}{ * the png\_controlp field 'opaque' to NULL (or, safer, memset the whole thing.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2980 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2981 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_STDIO\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2982 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(234, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, png\_image\_begin\_read\_from\_file, (png\_imagep \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__gui__basics-accessibility_ggaf1349587ab6cac7e882cd63e1976682ca78805a221a988e79ef3f42d7c5bfd418}{image}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{2983    \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *file\_name));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2984    \textcolor{comment}{/* The named file is opened for read and the image header is filled in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2985 \textcolor{comment}{    * from the PNG header in the file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2986 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2987 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2988 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(235, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, png\_image\_begin\_read\_from\_stdio, (png\_imagep \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__gui__basics-accessibility_ggaf1349587ab6cac7e882cd63e1976682ca78805a221a988e79ef3f42d7c5bfd418}{image}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{2989    FILE* file));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2990    \textcolor{comment}{/* The PNG header is read from the stdio FILE object. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2991 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* STDIO */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2992 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2993 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(236, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, png\_image\_begin\_read\_from\_memory, (png\_imagep \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__gui__basics-accessibility_ggaf1349587ab6cac7e882cd63e1976682ca78805a221a988e79ef3f42d7c5bfd418}{image}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{2994    \mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_aa2688aa7a3bd08819701a744f9a5716c}{png\_const\_voidp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_a3a5cfcada98dcfb74023a94251b8345b}{memory}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_a441d79156826d7dfbf89100bb934a38d}{size}}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2995    \textcolor{comment}{/* The PNG header is read from the given memory buffer. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2996 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2997 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(237, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, png\_image\_finish\_read, (png\_imagep \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__gui__basics-accessibility_ggaf1349587ab6cac7e882cd63e1976682ca78805a221a988e79ef3f42d7c5bfd418}{image}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{2998    \mbox{\hyperlink{structpng__color__struct}{png\_const\_colorp}} background, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *buffer, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngrutil_8c_a1f5cf5f6a913e237d8a9a7c0a6ea1714}{png\_int\_32}} row\_stride,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2999    \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *colormap));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3000    \textcolor{comment}{/* Finish reading the image into the supplied buffer and clean up the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3001 \textcolor{comment}{    * png\_image structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3002 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3003 \textcolor{comment}{    * row\_stride is the step, in byte or 2-\/byte units as appropriate,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3004 \textcolor{comment}{    * between adjacent rows.  A positive stride indicates that the top-\/most row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3005 \textcolor{comment}{    * is first in the buffer -\/ the normal top-\/down arrangement.  A negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3006 \textcolor{comment}{    * stride indicates that the bottom-\/most row is first in the buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3007 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3008 \textcolor{comment}{    * background need only be supplied if an alpha channel must be removed from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3009 \textcolor{comment}{    * a png\_byte format and the removal is to be done by compositing on a solid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3010 \textcolor{comment}{    * color; otherwise it may be NULL and any composition will be done directly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3011 \textcolor{comment}{    * onto the buffer.  The value is an sRGB color to use for the background,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3012 \textcolor{comment}{    * for grayscale output the green channel is used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3013 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3014 \textcolor{comment}{    * background must be supplied when an alpha channel must be removed from a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3015 \textcolor{comment}{    * single byte color-\/mapped output format, in other words if:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3016 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3017 \textcolor{comment}{    * 1) The original format from png\_image\_begin\_read\_from\_* had}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3018 \textcolor{comment}{    *    PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3019 \textcolor{comment}{    * 2) The format set by the application does not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3020 \textcolor{comment}{    * 3) The format set by the application has PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP set and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3021 \textcolor{comment}{    *    PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_LINEAR *not* set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3022 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3023 \textcolor{comment}{    * For linear output removing the alpha channel is always done by compositing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3024 \textcolor{comment}{    * on black and background is ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3025 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3026 \textcolor{comment}{    * colormap must be supplied when PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP is set.  It must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3027 \textcolor{comment}{    * be at least the size (in bytes) returned by PNG\_IMAGE\_COLORMAP\_SIZE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3028 \textcolor{comment}{    * image-\/>colormap\_entries will be updated to the actual number of entries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3029 \textcolor{comment}{    * written to the colormap; this may be less than the original value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3030 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3031 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3032 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(238, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}, png\_image\_free, (png\_imagep \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__gui__basics-accessibility_ggaf1349587ab6cac7e882cd63e1976682ca78805a221a988e79ef3f42d7c5bfd418}{image}}));}

\DoxyCodeLine{3037 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3038 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_WRITE\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3039 \textcolor{comment}{/* WRITE APIS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3040 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3041 \textcolor{comment}{ * For write you must initialize a png\_image structure to describe the image to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3042 \textcolor{comment}{ * be written.  To do this use memset to set the whole structure to 0 then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3043 \textcolor{comment}{ * initialize fields describing your image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3044 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3045 \textcolor{comment}{ * version: must be set to PNG\_IMAGE\_VERSION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3046 \textcolor{comment}{ * opaque: must be initialized to NULL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3047 \textcolor{comment}{ * width: image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3048 \textcolor{comment}{ * height: image height in rows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3049 \textcolor{comment}{ * format: the format of the data (image and color-\/map) you wish to write}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3050 \textcolor{comment}{ * flags: set to 0 unless one of the defined flags applies; set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3051 \textcolor{comment}{ *    PNG\_IMAGE\_FLAG\_COLORSPACE\_NOT\_sRGB for color format images where the RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3052 \textcolor{comment}{ *    values do not correspond to the colors in sRGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3053 \textcolor{comment}{ * colormap\_entries: set to the number of entries in the color-\/map (0 to 256)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3054 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3055 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_SIMPLIFIED\_WRITE\_STDIO\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3056 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(239, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, png\_image\_write\_to\_file, (png\_imagep \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__gui__basics-accessibility_ggaf1349587ab6cac7e882cd63e1976682ca78805a221a988e79ef3f42d7c5bfd418}{image}},}

\DoxyCodeLine{3066 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3067 \textcolor{comment}{/* With all write APIs if image is in one of the linear formats with 16-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3068 \textcolor{comment}{ * data then setting convert\_to\_8\_bit will cause the output to be an 8-\/bit PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3069 \textcolor{comment}{ * gamma encoded according to the sRGB specification, otherwise a 16-\/bit linear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3070 \textcolor{comment}{ * encoded PNG file is written.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3071 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3072 \textcolor{comment}{ * With color-\/mapped data formats the colormap parameter point to a color-\/map}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3073 \textcolor{comment}{ * with at least image-\/>colormap\_entries encoded in the specified format.  If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3074 \textcolor{comment}{ * the format is linear the written PNG color-\/map will be converted to sRGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3075 \textcolor{comment}{ * regardless of the convert\_to\_8\_bit flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3076 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3077 \textcolor{comment}{ * With all APIs row\_stride is handled as in the read APIs -\/ it is the spacing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3078 \textcolor{comment}{ * from one row to the next in component sized units (1 or 2 bytes) and if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3079 \textcolor{comment}{ * negative indicates a bottom-\/up row layout in the buffer.  If row\_stride is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3080 \textcolor{comment}{ * zero, libpng will calculate it for you from the image width and number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3081 \textcolor{comment}{ * channels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3082 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3083 \textcolor{comment}{ * Note that the write API does not support interlacing, sub-\/8-\/bit pixels or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3084 \textcolor{comment}{ * most ancillary chunks.  If you need to write text chunks (e.g. for copyright}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3085 \textcolor{comment}{ * notices) you need to use one of the other APIs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3086 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3087 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3088 \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_acf483e36ae60e767ba2401612346caee}{PNG\_EXPORT}}(245, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, png\_image\_write\_to\_memory, (png\_imagep \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__gui__basics-accessibility_ggaf1349587ab6cac7e882cd63e1976682ca78805a221a988e79ef3f42d7c5bfd418}{image}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_a3a5cfcada98dcfb74023a94251b8345b}{memory}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{3089    \mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a5f4e523d0194e10bd008d93b593ea989}{png\_alloc\_size\_t}} * \mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_af21b002e402fd844f1767dc3e7e92756}{PNG\_RESTRICT}} memory\_bytes, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} convert\_to\_8\_bit,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3090    \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *buffer, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngrutil_8c_a1f5cf5f6a913e237d8a9a7c0a6ea1714}{png\_int\_32}} row\_stride, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *colormap));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3091    \textcolor{comment}{/* Write the image to the given memory buffer.  The function both writes the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3092 \textcolor{comment}{    * whole PNG data stream to *memory and updates *memory\_bytes with the count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3093 \textcolor{comment}{    * of bytes written.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3094 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3095 \textcolor{comment}{    * 'memory' may be NULL.  In this case *memory\_bytes is not read however on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3096 \textcolor{comment}{    * success the number of bytes which would have been written will still be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3097 \textcolor{comment}{    * stored in *memory\_bytes.  On failure *memory\_bytes will contain 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3098 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3099 \textcolor{comment}{    * If 'memory' is not NULL it must point to memory[*memory\_bytes] of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3100 \textcolor{comment}{    * writeable memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3101 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3102 \textcolor{comment}{    * If the function returns success memory[*memory\_bytes] (if 'memory' is not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3103 \textcolor{comment}{    * NULL) contains the written PNG data.  *memory\_bytes will always be less}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3104 \textcolor{comment}{    * than or equal to the original value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3105 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3106 \textcolor{comment}{    * If the function returns false and *memory\_bytes was not changed an error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3107 \textcolor{comment}{    * occurred during write.  If *memory\_bytes was changed, or is not 0 if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3108 \textcolor{comment}{    * 'memory' was NULL, the write would have succeeded but for the memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3109 \textcolor{comment}{    * buffer being too small.  *memory\_bytes contains the required number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3110 \textcolor{comment}{    * bytes and will be bigger that the original value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3111 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3112 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3113 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_image\_write\_get\_memory\_size(image, size, convert\_to\_8\_bit, buffer,\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3114 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   row\_stride, colormap)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3115 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   png\_image\_write\_to\_memory(\&(image), 0, \&(size), convert\_to\_8\_bit, buffer,\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3116 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         row\_stride, colormap)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3117    \textcolor{comment}{/* Return the amount of memory in 'size' required to compress this image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3118 \textcolor{comment}{    * The png\_image structure 'image' must be filled in as in the above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3119 \textcolor{comment}{    * function and must not be changed before the actual write call, the buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3120 \textcolor{comment}{    * and all other parameters must also be identical to that in the final}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3121 \textcolor{comment}{    * write call.  The 'size' variable need not be initialized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3122 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3123 \textcolor{comment}{    * NOTE: the macro returns true/false, if false is returned 'size' will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3124 \textcolor{comment}{    * set to zero and the write failed and probably will fail if tried again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3125 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3126 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3127 \textcolor{comment}{/* You can pre-\/allocate the buffer by making sure it is of sufficient size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3128 \textcolor{comment}{ * regardless of the amount of compression achieved.  The buffer size will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3129 \textcolor{comment}{ * always be bigger than the original image and it will never be filled.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3130 \textcolor{comment}{ * following macros are provided to assist in allocating the buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3131 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3132 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_DATA\_SIZE(image) (PNG\_IMAGE\_SIZE(image)+(image).height)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3133    \textcolor{comment}{/* The number of uncompressed bytes in the PNG byte encoding of the image;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3134 \textcolor{comment}{    * uncompressing the PNG IDAT data will give this number of bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3135 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3136 \textcolor{comment}{    * NOTE: while PNG\_IMAGE\_SIZE cannot overflow for an image in memory this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3137 \textcolor{comment}{    * macro can because of the extra bytes used in the PNG byte encoding.  You}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3138 \textcolor{comment}{    * need to avoid this macro if your image size approaches 2\string^30 in width or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3139 \textcolor{comment}{    * height.  The same goes for the remainder of these macros; they all produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3140 \textcolor{comment}{    * bigger numbers than the actual in-\/memory image size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3141 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3142 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_ZLIB\_MAX\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3143 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_ZLIB\_MAX\_SIZE(b) ((b)+(((b)+7U)>>3)+(((b)+63U)>>6)+11U)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3144    \textcolor{comment}{/* An upper bound on the number of compressed bytes given 'b' uncompressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3145 \textcolor{comment}{    * bytes.  This is based on deflateBounds() in zlib; different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3146 \textcolor{comment}{    * implementations of zlib compression may conceivably produce more data so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3147 \textcolor{comment}{    * if your zlib implementation is not zlib itself redefine this macro}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3148 \textcolor{comment}{    * appropriately.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3149 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3150 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3151 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3152 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_COMPRESSED\_SIZE\_MAX(image)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3153 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   PNG\_ZLIB\_MAX\_SIZE((png\_alloc\_size\_t)PNG\_IMAGE\_DATA\_SIZE(image))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3154    \textcolor{comment}{/* An upper bound on the size of the data in the PNG IDAT chunks. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3155 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3156 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_PNG\_SIZE\_MAX\_(image, image\_size)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3157 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((8U}\textcolor{comment}{/*sig*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+25U}\textcolor{comment}{/*IHDR*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+16U}\textcolor{comment}{/*gAMA*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+44U}\textcolor{comment}{/*cHRM*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+12U}\textcolor{comment}{/*IEND*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3158 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    (((image).format\&PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_COLORMAP)?}\textcolor{comment}{/*colormap: PLTE, tRNS*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3159 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    12U+3U*(image).colormap\_entries}\textcolor{comment}{/*PLTE data*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3160 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    (((image).format\&PNG\_FORMAT\_FLAG\_ALPHA)?\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3161 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    12U}\textcolor{comment}{/*tRNS*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+(image).colormap\_entries:0U):0U)+\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3162 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    12U)+(12U*((image\_size)/PNG\_ZBUF\_SIZE))}\textcolor{comment}{/*IDAT*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{+(image\_size))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3163    \textcolor{comment}{/* A helper for the following macro; if your compiler cannot handle the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3164 \textcolor{comment}{    * following macro use this one with the result of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3165 \textcolor{comment}{    * PNG\_IMAGE\_COMPRESSED\_SIZE\_MAX(image) as the second argument (most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3166 \textcolor{comment}{    * compilers should handle this just fine.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3167 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3168 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3169 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IMAGE\_PNG\_SIZE\_MAX(image)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3170 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   PNG\_IMAGE\_PNG\_SIZE\_MAX\_(image, PNG\_IMAGE\_COMPRESSED\_SIZE\_MAX(image))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3171    \textcolor{comment}{/* An upper bound on the total length of the PNG data stream for 'image'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3172 \textcolor{comment}{    * The result is of type png\_alloc\_size\_t, on 32-\/bit systems this may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3173 \textcolor{comment}{    * overflow even though PNG\_IMAGE\_DATA\_SIZE does not overflow; the write will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3174 \textcolor{comment}{    * run out of buffer space but return a corrected size which should work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3175 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3176 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* SIMPLIFIED\_WRITE */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3181 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3182 \textcolor{comment}{/*******************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3183 \textcolor{comment}{ * Section 6: IMPLEMENTATION OPTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3184 \textcolor{comment}{ *******************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3185 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3186 \textcolor{comment}{ * Support for arbitrary implementation-\/specific optimizations.  The API allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3187 \textcolor{comment}{ * particular options to be turned on or off.  'Option' is the number of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3188 \textcolor{comment}{ * option and 'onoff' is 0 (off) or non-\/0 (on).  The value returned is given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3189 \textcolor{comment}{ * by the PNG\_OPTION\_ defines below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3190 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3191 \textcolor{comment}{ * HARDWARE: normally hardware capabilities, such as the Intel SSE instructions,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3192 \textcolor{comment}{ *           are detected at run time, however sometimes it may be impossible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3193 \textcolor{comment}{ *           to do this in user mode, in which case it is necessary to discover}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3194 \textcolor{comment}{ *           the capabilities in an OS specific way.  Such capabilities are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3195 \textcolor{comment}{ *           listed here when libpng has support for them and must be turned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3196 \textcolor{comment}{ *           ON by the application if present.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3197 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3198 \textcolor{comment}{ * SOFTWARE: sometimes software optimizations actually result in performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3199 \textcolor{comment}{ *           decrease on some architectures or systems, or with some sets of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3200 \textcolor{comment}{ *           PNG images.  'Software' options allow such optimizations to be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3201 \textcolor{comment}{ *           selected at run time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3202 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3203 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_SET\_OPTION\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3204 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_API\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3205 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_ARM\_NEON   0 }\textcolor{comment}{/* HARDWARE: ARM Neon SIMD instructions supported */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3206 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3207 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_MAXIMUM\_INFLATE\_WINDOW 2 }\textcolor{comment}{/* SOFTWARE: force maximum window */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3208 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_SKIP\_sRGB\_CHECK\_PROFILE 4 }\textcolor{comment}{/* SOFTWARE: Check ICC profile for sRGB */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3209 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_MIPS\_MSA\_API\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3210 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_MIPS\_MSA   6 }\textcolor{comment}{/* HARDWARE: MIPS Msa SIMD instructions supported */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3211 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3212 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_IGNORE\_ADLER32 8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3213 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_POWERPC\_VSX\_API\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_POWERPC\_VSX   10 }\textcolor{comment}{/* HARDWARE: PowerPC VSX SIMD instructions supported */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3215 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3216 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_OPTION\_NEXT  12 }\textcolor{comment}{/* Next option -\/ numbers must be even */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3217 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3218 \textcolor{comment}{/* Return values: NOTE: there are four values and 'off' is *not* zero */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_OPTION\_UNSET   0 }\textcolor{comment}{/* Unset -\/ defaults to off */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3220 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_OPTION\_INVALID 1 }\textcolor{comment}{/* Option number out of range */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_OPTION\_OFF     2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_OPTION\_ON      3}}
